\# CHANGES_phase2_v2.md \## Phase 2 --- Smart Product Compare (Croma + Reliance Digital) \*Replaces CHANGES_phase2.md entirely. Use this version.\* \-\-- \## What Phase 2 Adds Five capabilities, each building on the previous: \`\`\` Step 0 Query Refinement User types vague query тЖТ Groq suggests precise alternatives Step 1 SerpAPI Search Refined query тЖТ Google Shopping тЖТ product URLs Step 2 User Selects Grid of result cards, user picks 2--5 to compare Step 3 Scraper Croma + Reliance Digital pages тЖТ price, rating, specs Step 4 AI Ideal Suggester Spec matrix тЖТ Gemini/Groq тЖТ suggested ideals + weights Step 5 User Confirms Edits suggestions тЖТ fires existing /api/calculate \`\`\` Firebase / caching тЖТ Phase 3. Not in this spec. \-\-- \## Files Created / Modified \| File \| Action \| \|\-\-\-\-\--\|\-\-\-\-\-\-\--\| \| \`backend/scrapers/cromaScraper.js\` \| CREATE \| \| \`backend/scrapers/relianceScraper.js\` \| CREATE \| \| \`backend/scrapers/index.js\` \| CREATE --- unified scraper router \| \| \`backend/server.js\` \| ADD --- \`/api/refine-query\`, \`/api/search\`, \`/api/scrape\` endpoints \| \| \`frontend/index.html\` \| ADD --- Tab 2 HTML \| \| \`frontend/script.js\` \| ADD --- Phase 2 functions at bottom \| \| \`frontend/styles.css\` \| ADD --- Phase 2 styles at bottom \| DO NOT modify: \`decisionLogic.js\`, \`visualizer_prototype.html\`, any existing manual tab code, existing \`/api/preprocess\`, \`/api/calculate\` routes. \-\-- \## npm packages to install after applying \`\`\`bash cd backend npm install cheerio node-fetch \`\`\` \-\-- \## NEW FILE: \`backend/scrapers/cromaScraper.js\` \`\`\`js // cromaScraper.js // Scrapes croma.com product pages. // Croma is server-rendered --- no headless browser needed. // SELECTOR VERIFICATION NOTE: If any selector returns empty on first run, // inspect the live page in Chrome DevTools and update the selector here. const cheerio = require(\'cheerio\'); const HEADERS = { \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\', \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,\*/\*;q=0.8\', \'Accept-Language\': \'en-IN,en;q=0.9\', \'Accept-Encoding\': \'gzip, deflate, br\', \'Connection\': \'keep-alive\', }; function normaliseCromaUrl(url) { try { const u = new URL(url.trim()); if (!u.hostname.includes(\'croma.com\')) { throw new Error(\'Not a croma.com URL\'); } // Remove query params, keep clean path return { url: \`https://www.croma.com\${u.pathname}\`, source: \'croma\' }; } catch (e) { throw new Error(\`Invalid Croma URL: \${url}\`); } } async function scrapeCroma(rawUrl) { const { url } = normaliseCromaUrl(rawUrl); const fetch = (await import(\'node-fetch\')).default; const response = await fetch(url, { headers: HEADERS, timeout: 12000 }); if (!response.ok) throw new Error(\`HTTP \${response.status} from Croma\`); const html = await response.text(); const \$ = cheerio.load(html); // тФАтФА CAPTCHA / bot detection тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА if (\$(\'body\').text().toLowerCase().includes(\'access denied\') \|\| \$(\'title\').text().toLowerCase().includes(\'access denied\')) { throw new Error(\'Croma returned access denied. Try again later.\'); } // тФАтФА Product name тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА // Primary selectors --- verified against croma.com structure as of Feb 2026 // If empty: open page in Chrome тЖТ right-click product title тЖТ Inspect тЖТ copy selector const name = \$(\'h1.pdp-title\').first().text().trim() \|\| \$(\'h1\[class\*=\"product-title\"\]\').first().text().trim() \|\| \$(\'h1\').first().text().trim() \|\| \'Unknown Product\'; // тФАтФА Price тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const priceSelectors = \[ \'.pdp-offer-price\', \'\[data-testid=\"offer-price\"\]\', \'.offer-price\', \'.final-price\', \'\[class\*=\"offer-price\"\]\', \'\[class\*=\"final-price\"\]\', \]; let priceRaw = \'\'; for (const sel of priceSelectors) { priceRaw = \$(sel).first().text().trim(); if (priceRaw) break; } const priceNum = parseFloat(priceRaw.replace(/\[тВ╣,\\s\]/g, \'\')); const price = isNaN(priceNum) ? null : priceNum; // тФАтФА Rating тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const ratingSelectors = \[ \'.pdp-rating .rating-value\', \'\[class\*=\"rating-value\"\]\', \'.star-rating span\', \'\[data-testid=\"rating\"\]\', \]; let ratingRaw = \'\'; for (const sel of ratingSelectors) { ratingRaw = \$(sel).first().text().trim(); if (ratingRaw) break; } const ratingNum = parseFloat(ratingRaw); const rating = isNaN(ratingNum) ? null : ratingNum; // тФАтФА Review count тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const reviewRaw = \$(\'\[class\*=\"review-count\"\]\').first().text().trim() \|\| \$(\'\[class\*=\"rating-count\"\]\').first().text().trim() \|\| \'\'; const reviewMatch = reviewRaw.match(/\[\\d,\]+/); const reviewCount = reviewMatch ? parseInt(reviewMatch\[0\].replace(/,/g, \'\'), 10) : null; // тФАтФА Tech specs table тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const specs = {}; // Primary: specification table rows \$(\'table.specification-table tr, .pdp-specs table tr, \[class\*=\"spec\"\] table tr\').each((\_, row) =\> { const key = \$(row).find(\'td:first-child, th\').first().text().trim(); const val = \$(row).find(\'td:last-child\').first().text().trim().replace(/\\s+/g, \' \'); if (key && val && key !== val && key.length \< 80) { specs\[key\] = val; } }); // Fallback: definition lists if (Object.keys(specs).length === 0) { \$(\'dl.specification dt, \[class\*=\"spec-key\"\]\').each((idx, el) =\> { const key = \$(el).text().trim(); const val = \$(el).next(\'dd, \[class\*=\"spec-value\"\]\').text().trim(); if (key && val) specs\[key\] = val; }); } // тФАтФА Product image тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const image = \$(\'img.pdp-image\').first().attr(\'src\') \|\| \$(\'img\[class\*=\"product-image\"\]\').first().attr(\'src\') \|\| \$(\'.pdp-gallery img\').first().attr(\'src\') \|\| null; return { name, price, rating, reviewCount, specs, image, url, source: \'croma\', }; } module.exports = { scrapeCroma, normaliseCromaUrl }; \`\`\` \-\-- \## NEW FILE: \`backend/scrapers/relianceScraper.js\` \`\`\`js // relianceScraper.js // Scrapes reliancedigital.in product pages. // Also server-rendered, minimal bot protection. const cheerio = require(\'cheerio\'); const HEADERS = { \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\', \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,\*/\*;q=0.8\', \'Accept-Language\': \'en-IN,en;q=0.9\', \'Connection\': \'keep-alive\', }; function normaliseRelianceUrl(url) { try { const u = new URL(url.trim()); if (!u.hostname.includes(\'reliancedigital.in\')) { throw new Error(\'Not a reliancedigital.in URL\'); } return { url: \`https://www.reliancedigital.in\${u.pathname}\`, source: \'reliance\' }; } catch (e) { throw new Error(\`Invalid Reliance Digital URL: \${url}\`); } } async function scrapeReliance(rawUrl) { const { url } = normaliseRelianceUrl(rawUrl); const fetch = (await import(\'node-fetch\')).default; const response = await fetch(url, { headers: HEADERS, timeout: 12000 }); if (!response.ok) throw new Error(\`HTTP \${response.status} from Reliance Digital\`); const html = await response.text(); const \$ = cheerio.load(html); // тФАтФА Product name тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const name = \$(\'h1.product-name\').first().text().trim() \|\| \$(\'h1\[class\*=\"pdp-name\"\]\').first().text().trim() \|\| \$(\'h1\').first().text().trim() \|\| \'Unknown Product\'; // тФАтФА Price тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const priceSelectors = \[ \'.price-value\', \'.offer-price\', \'\[class\*=\"selling-price\"\]\', \'\[class\*=\"offer-price\"\]\', \'span.price\', \]; let priceRaw = \'\'; for (const sel of priceSelectors) { priceRaw = \$(sel).first().text().trim(); if (priceRaw) break; } const priceNum = parseFloat(priceRaw.replace(/\[тВ╣,\\s\]/g, \'\')); const price = isNaN(priceNum) ? null : priceNum; // тФАтФА Rating тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const ratingRaw = \$(\'\[class\*=\"rating-value\"\]\').first().text().trim() \|\| \$(\'\[class\*=\"average-rating\"\]\').first().text().trim() \|\| \'\'; const ratingNum = parseFloat(ratingRaw); const rating = isNaN(ratingNum) ? null : ratingNum; // тФАтФА Review count тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const reviewRaw = \$(\'\[class\*=\"review-count\"\]\').first().text().trim() \|\| \$(\'\[class\*=\"total-review\"\]\').first().text().trim() \|\| \'\'; const reviewMatch = reviewRaw.match(/\[\\d,\]+/); const reviewCount = reviewMatch ? parseInt(reviewMatch\[0\].replace(/,/g, \'\'), 10) : null; // тФАтФА Tech specs table тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const specs = {}; \$(\'.specifications-table tr, .tab-pane table tr, \[class\*=\"spec\"\] tr\').each((\_, row) =\> { const cells = \$(row).find(\'td\'); if (cells.length \>= 2) { const key = \$(cells\[0\]).text().trim(); const val = \$(cells\[1\]).text().trim().replace(/\\s+/g, \' \'); if (key && val && key.length \< 80) specs\[key\] = val; } }); if (Object.keys(specs).length === 0) { \$(\'\[class\*=\"spec-label\"\], \[class\*=\"spec-name\"\]\').each((\_, el) =\> { const key = \$(el).text().trim(); const val = \$(el) .closest(\'li, tr, div\') .find(\'\[class\*=\"spec-value\"\], \[class\*=\"spec-data\"\]\') .first() .text() .trim(); if (key && val) specs\[key\] = val; }); } // тФАтФА Product image тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const image = \$(\'img.product-image\').first().attr(\'src\') \|\| \$(\'img\[class\*=\"pdp-image\"\]\').first().attr(\'src\') \|\| null; return { name, price, rating, reviewCount, specs, image, url, source: \'reliance\', }; } module.exports = { scrapeReliance, normaliseRelianceUrl }; \`\`\` \-\-- \## NEW FILE: \`backend/scrapers/index.js\` \`\`\`js // scrapers/index.js // Routes a URL to the correct scraper based on domain. const { scrapeCroma, normaliseCromaUrl } = require(\'./cromaScraper\'); const { scrapeReliance, normaliseRelianceUrl } = require(\'./relianceScraper\'); function detectSource(url) { if (url.includes(\'croma.com\')) return \'croma\'; if (url.includes(\'reliancedigital.in\')) return \'reliance\'; return null; } async function scrapeProduct(url) { const source = detectSource(url); if (!source) { throw new Error( \`Unsupported URL. Paste a croma.com or reliancedigital.in product URL.\` ); } if (source === \'croma\') return scrapeCroma(url); if (source === \'reliance\') return scrapeReliance(url); } async function scrapeProducts(urls) { const delay = (ms) =\> new Promise((r) =\> setTimeout(r, ms)); const results = \[\]; for (let i = 0; i \< urls.length; i++) { try { const data = await scrapeProduct(urls\[i\]); results.push({ success: true, data }); } catch (e) { results.push({ success: false, url: urls\[i\], error: e.message }); } if (i \< urls.length - 1) await delay(600); } return results; } module.exports = { scrapeProducts, detectSource }; \`\`\` \-\-- \## CHANGE: \`backend/server.js\` --- Add 3 new endpoints Add the following block after the existing \`/api/calculate\` route, before \`app.listen(\...)\`. \`\`\`js // тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА // PHASE 2 --- Query Refinement, Search, Scrape // тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА const { scrapeProducts } = require(\'./scrapers/index\'); // тФАтФА 1. Query Refinement тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА // Takes a vague user query and returns 3--4 refined search suggestions. // Falls back to a template object when AI fails. app.post(\'/api/refine-query\', async (req, res) =\> { const { query } = req.body; if (!query \|\| query.trim().length \< 2) { return res.status(400).json({ error: \'Query too short.\' }); } const prompt = \`A user wants to compare products online. Their search query is: \"\${query}\" This query may be vague, a brand name only, or a category name only. Your job is to suggest 3--4 refined, specific search queries that would return better product comparison results on an Indian e-commerce site. Rules: - Be specific: include category, budget range, or key feature - Use Indian context (тВ╣ for prices, Indian market context) - If the query mentions a brand: generate queries with that brand + specific products - If the query mentions a category: generate queries with budget ranges - Keep each suggestion under 60 characters Also detect what template fields are needed if the user wants to manually specify their search instead. Output ONLY a raw JSON object. No markdown, no backticks. Format: { \"suggestions\": \[ \"Samsung Galaxy phones under тВ╣20,000\", \"Samsung Galaxy S24 series India\", \"Samsung budget smartphones 2024\" \], \"template\": { \"fields\": \[\"product_type\", \"budget\"\], \"placeholder\": \"e.g. Samsung phones under тВ╣25,000\" } }\`; // Try Groq first (faster for short outputs) try { const groqKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY; if (!groqKey) throw new Error(\'No Groq key\'); const response = await fetch(\'https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions\', { method: \'POST\', headers: { Authorization: \`Bearer \${groqKey}\`, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\', }, body: JSON.stringify({ model: \'llama-3.3-70b-versatile\', max_tokens: 300, temperature: 0.4, messages: \[{ role: \'user\', content: prompt }\], }), }); if (!response.ok) throw new Error(\`Groq \${response.status}\`); const data = await response.json(); const raw = data.choices?.\[0\]?.message?.content?.trim(); if (!raw) throw new Error(\'Empty response\'); const match = raw.match(/\\{\[\\s\\S\]\*\\}/); if (!match) throw new Error(\'No JSON found\'); const parsed = JSON.parse(match\[0\]); return res.json({ \...parsed, source: \'groq\' }); } catch (e) { console.log(\'Groq refine failed:\', e.message); } // Try Gemini fallback try { const geminiKey = process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY; if (!geminiKey) throw new Error(\'No Gemini key\'); const url = \`https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.0-flash:generateContent?key=\${geminiKey}\`; const response = await fetch(url, { method: \'POST\', headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }, body: JSON.stringify({ contents: \[{ parts: \[{ text: prompt }\] }\], generationConfig: { maxOutputTokens: 300, temperature: 0.4 }, }), }); if (!response.ok) throw new Error(\`Gemini \${response.status}\`); const data = await response.json(); const raw = data.candidates?.\[0\]?.content?.parts?.\[0\]?.text?.trim(); if (!raw) throw new Error(\'Empty response\'); const match = raw.match(/\\{\[\\s\\S\]\*\\}/); if (!match) throw new Error(\'No JSON found\'); const parsed = JSON.parse(match\[0\]); return res.json({ \...parsed, source: \'gemini\' }); } catch (e) { console.log(\'Gemini refine failed:\', e.message); } // Hard fallback: keyword-based template const lower = query.toLowerCase(); const isBrand = /samsung\|apple\|sony\|lg\|oneplus\|realme\|redmi\|oppo\|vivo\|boat\|jbl\|bose/i.test(query); const isCategory = /phone\|laptop\|earphone\|speaker\|tv\|watch\|tablet\|camera/i.test(query); const fallbackSuggestions = isBrand ? \[ \`\${query} smartphones under тВ╣20,000\`, \`\${query} smartphones under тВ╣30,000\`, \`\${query} flagship phones 2024\`, \] : isCategory ? \[ \`Best \${query} under тВ╣10,000\`, \`Best \${query} under тВ╣20,000\`, \`Top rated \${query} India 2024\`, \] : \[ \`\${query} under тВ╣15,000\`, \`\${query} under тВ╣25,000\`, \`Best \${query} India\`, \]; res.json({ suggestions: fallbackSuggestions, template: { fields: \[\'product_type\', \'budget\'\], placeholder: \`e.g. \${query} under тВ╣\_\_\_\_\_\`, }, source: \'fallback\', }); }); // тФАтФА 2. SerpAPI Product Search тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА app.post(\'/api/search\', async (req, res) =\> { const { query } = req.body; if (!query) return res.status(400).json({ error: \'Query required.\' }); const serpKey = process.env.SERPAPI_KEY; if (!serpKey) { return res.status(503).json({ error: \'SERPAPI_KEY not configured.\', hint: \'Add SERPAPI_KEY to your .env file. Get a free key at serpapi.com\', }); } try { const fetch = (await import(\'node-fetch\')).default; // Search Google Shopping, biased toward Indian results const searchUrl = \`https://serpapi.com/search.json?q=\${encodeURIComponent(query)}&tbm=shop&gl=in&hl=en&api_key=\${serpKey}&num=8\`; const response = await fetch(searchUrl, { timeout: 10000 }); if (!response.ok) throw new Error(\`SerpAPI \${response.status}\`); const data = await response.json(); if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error); const results = (data.shopping_results \|\| \[\]).slice(0, 8).map((item) =\> ({ title: item.title, price: item.price, priceNum: item.extracted_price \|\| null, source: item.source, link: item.link, thumbnail: item.thumbnail, rating: item.rating \|\| null, reviews: item.reviews \|\| null, })); // Filter to only Croma and Reliance Digital results if available // Fall back to all results if neither is present const preferred = results.filter( (r) =\> r.source?.toLowerCase().includes(\'croma\') \|\| r.source?.toLowerCase().includes(\'reliance\') ); res.json({ results: preferred.length \>= 2 ? preferred : results, query, total: results.length, }); } catch (e) { console.error(\'Search error:\', e.message); res.status(500).json({ error: e.message }); } }); // тФАтФА 3. Scraper + AI Ideal Suggester тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА app.post(\'/api/scrape\', async (req, res) =\> { const { urls } = req.body; if (!Array.isArray(urls) \|\| urls.length \< 2 \|\| urls.length \> 5) { return res.status(400).json({ error: \'Provide between 2 and 5 product URLs.\' }); } const scrapeResults = await scrapeProducts(urls); const failed = scrapeResults.filter((r) =\> !r.success); const succeeded = scrapeResults.filter((r) =\> r.success).map((r) =\> r.data); if (succeeded.length \< 2) { return res.status(422).json({ error: \'Could not scrape enough products (need at least 2).\', failures: failed.map((f) =\> ({ url: f.url, reason: f.error })), }); } // Find common spec keys (appear in тЙе50% of products) const specKeyCounts = {}; for (const p of succeeded) { for (const key of Object.keys(p.specs)) { specKeyCounts\[key\] = (specKeyCounts\[key\] \|\| 0) + 1; } } const commonSpecs = Object.entries(specKeyCounts) .filter((\[\_, count\]) =\> count \>= Math.max(2, Math.floor(succeeded.length \* 0.5))) .sort((a, b) =\> b\[1\] - a\[1\]) .slice(0, 8) .map((\[key\]) =\> key); const hasPrice = succeeded.some((p) =\> p.price !== null); const hasRating = succeeded.some((p) =\> p.rating !== null); const alwaysCriteria = \[ \...(hasPrice ? \[\'Price\'\] : \[\]), \...(hasRating ? \[\'Rating\'\] : \[\]), \]; const allCriteria = \[\...alwaysCriteria, \...commonSpecs\]; // Build products_data matrix const products_data = {}; for (const p of succeeded) { const shortName = p.name.length \> 40 ? p.name.substring(0, 38) + \'\...\' : p.name; products_data\[shortName\] = {}; if (hasPrice) products_data\[shortName\]\[\'Price\'\] = p.price ?? null; if (hasRating) products_data\[shortName\]\[\'Rating\'\] = p.rating ?? null; for (const spec of commonSpecs) { products_data\[shortName\]\[spec\] = p.specs\[spec\] ?? null; } } // AI ideal suggestions const suggestions = await getAISuggestions( buildIdealSuggestionPrompt(products_data, allCriteria), allCriteria, products_data ); res.json({ products: succeeded.map((p) =\> ({ name: p.name, shortName: p.name.length \> 40 ? p.name.substring(0, 38) + \'\...\' : p.name, price: p.price, rating: p.rating, reviewCount: p.reviewCount, image: p.image, url: p.url, source: p.source, })), criteria: allCriteria, products_data, suggestions, failures: failed.map((f) =\> ({ url: f.url, reason: f.error })), }); }); // тФАтФА AI Ideal Suggestion helpers (shared) тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА function buildIdealSuggestionPrompt(products_data, criteria) { const productNames = Object.keys(products_data); const dataStr = productNames .map((name) =\> { const vals = criteria.map((c) =\> \`\${c}: \${products_data\[name\]\[c\] ?? \'N/A\'}\`).join(\', \'); return \`\${name}: { \${vals} }\`; }) .join(\'\\n\'); return \`You are a consumer advisor. Given these products and their values, suggest ideal target values and importance weights for a decision comparison. Products: \${dataStr} For each criterion, return: - ideal: the best target value a buyer would want (number only) - weight: importance from 1 (low) to 5 (high) - direction: \"lower\" if lower is better (Price, Weight), \"higher\" if higher is better (Rating, Battery) - reasoning: one short sentence Rules: - For Price: ideal = lowest price among options or slightly below - For Rating: ideal = 4.5 or 5.0 - For specs with units (e.g. \"30 hours\"): extract the number only Output ONLY raw JSON. No markdown, no backticks. Format: { \"CriterionName\": { \"ideal\": 24990, \"weight\": 4, \"direction\": \"lower\", \"reasoning\": \"\...\" }, \... }\`; } async function getAISuggestions(prompt, criteria) { const fallback = {}; for (const c of criteria) { const direction = \[\'price\', \'weight\', \'cost\'\].some((w) =\> c.toLowerCase().includes(w)) ? \'lower\' : \'higher\'; fallback\[c\] = { ideal: null, weight: 3, direction, reasoning: \'AI suggestion unavailable.\' }; } try { const groqKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY; if (!groqKey) throw new Error(\'No Groq key\'); const response = await fetch(\'https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions\', { method: \'POST\', headers: { Authorization: \`Bearer \${groqKey}\`, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }, body: JSON.stringify({ model: \'llama-3.3-70b-versatile\', max_tokens: 800, temperature: 0.3, messages: \[{ role: \'user\', content: prompt }\], }), }); if (!response.ok) throw new Error(\`Groq \${response.status}\`); const data = await response.json(); const raw = data.choices?.\[0\]?.message?.content?.trim(); const match = raw?.match(/\\{\[\\s\\S\]\*\\}/); if (!match) throw new Error(\'No JSON\'); return { \...fallback, \...JSON.parse(match\[0\]) }; } catch (e) { console.log(\'Groq suggestion failed:\', e.message); } try { const geminiKey = process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY; if (!geminiKey) throw new Error(\'No Gemini key\'); const url = \`https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.0-flash:generateContent?key=\${geminiKey}\`; const response = await fetch(url, { method: \'POST\', headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }, body: JSON.stringify({ contents: \[{ parts: \[{ text: prompt }\] }\], generationConfig: { maxOutputTokens: 800, temperature: 0.3 }, }), }); if (!response.ok) throw new Error(\`Gemini \${response.status}\`); const data = await response.json(); const raw = data.candidates?.\[0\]?.content?.parts?.\[0\]?.text?.trim(); const match = raw?.match(/\\{\[\\s\\S\]\*\\}/); if (!match) throw new Error(\'No JSON\'); return { \...fallback, \...JSON.parse(match\[0\]) }; } catch (e) { console.log(\'Gemini suggestion failed:\', e.message); } return fallback; } \`\`\` \-\-- \## CHANGE: \`frontend/index.html\` --- Add Tab 2 \### Step A --- Add tab bar immediately after \`\<body\>\` \`\`\`html \<div id=\"tab-bar\"\> \<button class=\"tab-btn active\" id=\"tab-manual-btn\" onclick=\"switchTab(\'manual\')\"\> тЬПя╕П Manual Compare \</button\> \<button class=\"tab-btn\" id=\"tab-amazon-btn\" onclick=\"switchTab(\'smart\')\"\> ЁЯЫТ Smart Compare \</button\> \</div\> \`\`\` \### Step B --- Add \`id=\"tab-manual\"\` to the existing main container div Find the outermost \`\<div class=\"container\"\>\` that wraps all existing \`.step\` divs. Add \`id=\"tab-manual\"\` to it: \`\`\`html \<div class=\"container\" id=\"tab-manual\"\> \`\`\` \### Step C --- Add Tab 2 block after the closing \`\</div\>\` of \`tab-manual\` \`\`\`html \<!\-- тФАтФА TAB 2: Smart Compare тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА \--\> \<div id=\"tab-smart\" class=\"tab-content hidden\"\> \<div class=\"container\"\> \<!\-- Step 0: Query Input + Refinement \--\> \<div id=\"step-smart-search\" class=\"step active\"\> \<h2\>ЁЯЫТ Smart Compare\</h2\> \<p class=\"hint\" style=\"margin-bottom:20px;\"\> Search for any product. // тФАтФА Tab switching тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА function switchTab(tab) { document.getElementById(\'tab-manual\').classList.toggle(\'hidden\', tab !== \'manual\'); document.getElementById(\'tab-smart\').classList.toggle(\'hidden\', tab !== \'smart\'); document.getElementById(\'tab-manual-btn\').classList.toggle(\'active\', tab === \'manual\'); document.getElementById(\'tab-amazon-btn\').classList.toggle(\'active\', tab === \'smart\'); } // тФАтФА Step 0: Query Refinement тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА async function refineQuery() { const input = document.getElementById(\'smart-query-input\'); const query = input.value.trim(); const errorEl = document.getElementById(\'smart-search-error\'); errorEl.classList.add(\'hidden\'); if (!query \|\| query.length \< 2) { errorEl.textContent = \'тЪая╕П Please enter a search term.\'; errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); return; } smartState.query = query; showLoading(1); try { const res = await fetch(\'/api/refine-query\', { method: \'POST\', headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }, body: JSON.stringify({ query }), }); const data = await res.json(); hideLoading(); if (data.suggestions?.length \> 0) { renderSuggestions(data.suggestions, query); } else if (data.template) { renderTemplate(data.template, query); } } catch (e) { hideLoading(); // Network fail --- just proceed to search with original query await runSearch(query); } } function renderSuggestions(suggestions, originalQuery) { const panel = document.getElementById(\'smart-suggestions\'); const chips = document.getElementById(\'suggestion-chips\'); chips.innerHTML = \'\'; // Always show original query as first option \[originalQuery, \...suggestions\].forEach((s, idx) =\> { const chip = document.createElement(\'button\'); chip.className = \'suggestion-chip\' + (idx === 0 ? \' chip-original\' : \'\'); chip.textContent = idx === 0 ? \`\"\${s}\" (original)\` : s; chip.onclick = () =\> confirmAndSearch(s); chips.appendChild(chip); }); panel.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); document.getElementById(\'smart-template\').classList.add(\'hidden\'); } function renderTemplate(template, query) { const panel = document.getElementById(\'smart-template\'); const fields = document.getElementById(\'template-fields\'); fields.innerHTML = \'\'; template.fields.forEach((field) =\> { const label = field.replace(/\_/g, \' \'); const div = document.createElement(\'div\'); div.className = \'form-group\'; div.innerHTML = \` \<label\>\${label}:\</label\> \<input type=\"text\" id=\"tpl-\${field}\" placeholder=\"\${template.placeholder \|\| \'\'}\" /\> \`; fields.appendChild(div); }); panel.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); document.getElementById(\'smart-suggestions\').classList.add(\'hidden\'); } function buildFromTemplate() { const fields = document.querySelectorAll(\'#template-fields input\'); const parts = Array.from(fields) .map((f) =\> f.value.trim()) .filter(Boolean); if (!parts.length) return; const built = parts.join(\' \'); document.getElementById(\'smart-query-input\').value = built; confirmAndSearch(built); } function confirmAndSearch(query) { const confirmed = confirm(\`Search for: \"\${query}\"?\`); if (confirmed) runSearch(query); } // тФАтФА Step 1: Search тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА async function runSearch(query) { showLoading(1); const errorEl = document.getElementById(\'smart-search-error\'); errorEl.classList.add(\'hidden\'); try { const res = await fetch(\'/api/search\', { method: \'POST\', headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }, body: JSON.stringify({ query }), }); const data = await res.json(); hideLoading(); if (!res.ok) { errorEl.textContent = \`тЭМ \${data.error \|\| \'Search failed\'}\`; if (data.hint) errorEl.textContent += \` --- \${data.hint}\`; errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); return; } smartState.searchResults = data.results; renderSearchResults(data.results, query); showAmazonStep(\'step-smart-results\'); } catch (e) { hideLoading(); errorEl.textContent = \`тЭМ Network error: \${e.message}\`; errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); } } function renderSearchResults(results, query) { const grid = document.getElementById(\'smart-result-grid\'); const subtitle = document.getElementById(\'smart-results-subtitle\'); subtitle.textContent = \`Results for \"\${query}\" --- select 2--5 to compare.\`; grid.innerHTML = \'\'; if (!results.length) { grid.innerHTML = \'\<p style=\"color:#94a3b8;font-size:0.9rem;\"\>No results found. Try pasting URLs directly below.\</p\>\'; return; } results.forEach((r, idx) =\> { const card = document.createElement(\'div\'); card.className = \'search-result-card\'; card.dataset.url = r.link; card.innerHTML = \` \<label class=\"search-card-label\"\> \<input type=\"checkbox\" class=\"search-card-check\" value=\"\${r.link}\" /\> \<div class=\"search-card-inner\"\> \${r.thumbnail ? \`\<img src=\"\${r.thumbnail}\" class=\"search-thumb\" alt=\"\" /\>\` : \'\<div class=\"search-thumb-placeholder\"\>ЁЯУж\</div\>\'} \<div class=\"search-card-info\"\> \<div class=\"search-card-title\"\>\${r.title}\</div\> \<div class=\"search-card-meta\"\> \${r.price ? \`\<span class=\"search-price\"\>\${r.price}\</span\>\` : \'\'} \${r.rating ? \`\<span class=\"search-rating\"\>тШЕ \${r.rating}\</span\>\` : \'\'} \${r.source ? \`\<span class=\"search-source\"\>\${r.source}\</span\>\` : \'\'} \</div\> \</div\> \</div\> \</label\> \`; grid.appendChild(card); }); } // тФАтФА URL fallback field тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА function addSmartUrlField() { const container = document.getElementById(\'manual-url-inputs\'); const count = container.querySelectorAll(\'.smart-url-field\').length; if (count \>= 5) { alert(\'Maximum 5 URLs.\'); return; } const row = document.createElement(\'div\'); row.className = \'url-input-row\'; row.innerHTML = \` \<label\>URL \${count + 1}\</label\> \<input type=\"url\" class=\"smart-url-field\" placeholder=\"https://www.croma.com/\...\" /\> \`; container.appendChild(row); } // тФАтФА Step 2: Scrape selected тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА async function startSmartScrape() { const errorEl = document.getElementById(\'smart-scrape-error\'); errorEl.classList.add(\'hidden\'); // Collect checked search result URLs const checked = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(\'.search-card-check:checked\')) .map((cb) =\> cb.value); // Collect manually entered URLs const manualUrls = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(\'.smart-url-field\')) .map((i) =\> i.value.trim()) .filter(Boolean); const urls = \[\...new Set(\[\...checked, \...manualUrls\])\]; if (urls.length \< 2) { errorEl.textContent = \'тЪая╕П Select or paste at least 2 products to compare.\'; errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); return; } if (urls.length \> 5) { errorEl.textContent = \'тЪая╕П Maximum 5 products.\'; errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); return; } showLoading(1); try { const res = await fetch(\'/api/scrape\', { method: \'POST\', headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }, body: JSON.stringify({ urls }), }); const data = await res.json(); hideLoading(); if (!res.ok) { errorEl.textContent = \`тЭМ \${data.error}\`; errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); return; } smartState.scrapeResult = data; renderSmartPreview(data); showAmazonStep(\'step-smart-preview\'); } catch (e) { hideLoading(); errorEl.textContent = \`тЭМ \${e.message}\`; errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); } } // тФАтФА Render preview cards тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА function renderSmartPreview(data) { const container = document.getElementById(\'smart-preview-cards\'); container.innerHTML = \'\'; data.products.forEach((p) =\> { const card = document.createElement(\'div\'); card.className = \'amazon-preview-card\'; const sourceBadge = p.source === \'croma\' ? \'\<span style=\"background:#e8f5e9;color:#2e7d32;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;font-size:0.72rem;font-weight:700;\"\>Croma\</span\>\' : \'\<span style=\"background:#e3f2fd;color:#1565c0;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;font-size:0.72rem;font-weight:700;\"\>Reliance Digital\</span\>\'; card.innerHTML = \` \<div class=\"amazon-card-inner\"\> \${p.image ? \`\<img src=\"\${p.image}\" alt=\"\${p.name}\" class=\"amazon-thumb\" /\>\` : \'\<div class=\"amazon-thumb-placeholder\"\>ЁЯУж\</div\>\'} \<div class=\"amazon-card-info\"\> \<div class=\"amazon-card-name\"\>\${p.name} \${sourceBadge}\</div\> \<div class=\"amazon-card-meta\"\> \${p.price ? \`\<span class=\"amazon-price\"\>тВ╣\${p.price.toLocaleString(\'en-IN\')}\</span\>\` : \'\'} \${p.rating ? \`\<span class=\"amazon-rating\"\>тШЕ \${p.rating}\</span\>\` : \'\'} \</div\> \</div\> \</div\> \`; container.appendChild(card); }); if (data.failures?.length \> 0) { const fb = document.getElementById(\'smart-failures-block\'); fb.classList.remove(\'hidden\'); fb.innerHTML = \`\<div class=\"warning-alert\"\>тЪая╕П \${data.failures.length} URL(s) failed: \${data.failures.map((f) =\> f.reason).join(\', \')}\</div\>\`; } } // тФАтФА Step 3: Render AI ideal suggestions тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА function showSmartIdeals() { const { criteria, suggestions } = smartState.scrapeResult; const container = document.getElementById(\'smart-ideals-container\'); container.innerHTML = \'\'; criteria.forEach((criterion, idx) =\> { const s = suggestions\[criterion\] \|\| {}; const row = document.createElement(\'div\'); row.className = \'amazon-ideal-row\'; row.innerHTML = \` \<div class=\"amazon-ideal-header\"\> \<span class=\"amazon-ideal-name\"\>\${criterion}\</span\> \<span class=\"amazon-ideal-reasoning\"\>\${s.reasoning \|\| \'\'}\</span\> \</div\> \<div class=\"amazon-ideal-inputs\"\> \<div class=\"form-group\"\> \<label\>Ideal Value:\</label\> \<input type=\"number\" id=\"smart-ideal-\${idx}\" value=\"\${s.ideal ?? \'\'}\" step=\"any\" /\> \</div\> \<div class=\"form-group\"\> \<label\>Importance (1--5):\</label\> \<input type=\"number\" id=\"smart-weight-\${idx}\" value=\"\${s.weight ?? 3}\" min=\"1\" max=\"5\" /\> \</div\> \<div class=\"form-group\"\> \<label\>Better When:\</label\> \<select id=\"smart-direction-\${idx}\"\> \<option value=\"lower\" \${s.direction === \'lower\' ? \'selected\' : \'\'}\>Lower\</option\> \<option value=\"higher\" \${s.direction === \'higher\' ? \'selected\' : \'\'}\>Higher\</option\> \</select\> \</div\> \</div\> \`; container.appendChild(row); }); showAmazonStep(\'step-smart-ideals\'); } // тФАтФА Step 4: Run calculation тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА async function runSmartCalculation() { const { criteria, products_data } = smartState.scrapeResult; const ideals = \[\], weights = \[\], directions = \[\]; for (let i = 0; i \< criteria.length; i++) { const ideal = parseFloat(document.getElementById(\`smart-ideal-\${i}\`).value); const weight = parseFloat(document.getElementById(\`smart-weight-\${i}\`).value); const direction = document.getElementById(\`smart-direction-\${i}\`).value; if (isNaN(ideal)) { alert(\`тЪая╕П Enter ideal value for \"\${criteria\[i\]}\"\`); return; } if (weight \<= 0) { alert(\`тЪая╕П Importance for \"\${criteria\[i\]}\" must be positive.\`); return; } ideals.push(ideal); weights.push(weight); directions.push(direction === \'higher\' ? \'True\' : \'False\'); } // Replace nulls with column average const cleanData = {}; for (const \[product, vals\] of Object.entries(products_data)) { cleanData\[product\] = {}; for (let i = 0; i \< criteria.length; i++) { const c = criteria\[i\]; const raw = parseFloat(vals\[c\]); if (!isNaN(raw)) { cleanData\[product\]\[c\] = raw; } else { const colVals = Object.values(products_data) .map((v) =\> parseFloat(v\[c\])) .filter((n) =\> !isNaN(n)); cleanData\[product\]\[c\] = colVals.length ? colVals.reduce((a, b) =\> a + b, 0) / colVals.length : 5; } } } showLoading(2); try { const res = await fetch(\'/api/calculate\', { method: \'POST\', headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }, body: JSON.stringify({ products_data: cleanData, features: criteria, weights_raw: weights, ideals, directions, metadata: null, }), }); if (!res.ok) throw new Error(\'Calculation failed\'); const result = await res.json(); hideLoading(); // Redirect displayResults() output to smart results container const main = document.getElementById(\'results-container\'); const smartContainer = document.getElementById(\'smart-results-container\'); main.id = \'\_\_hidden\'; smartContainer.id = \'results-container\'; state.featureNames = criteria; state.ideals = ideals; displayResults(result); smartContainer.id = \'smart-results-container\'; main.id = \'results-container\'; showAmazonStep(\'step-smart-final\'); } catch (e) { hideLoading(); alert(\'тЭМ \' + e.message); } } // тФАтФА Navigation тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА function showAmazonStep(stepId) { document.querySelectorAll(\'#tab-smart .step\').forEach((s) =\> s.classList.remove(\'active\')); document.getElementById(stepId).classList.add(\'active\'); // Wire up ideals step when navigating to it if (stepId === \'step-smart-ideals\') showSmartIdeals(); } function resetSmart() { smartState = { query: \'\', searchResults: \[\], selectedUrls: \[\], scrapeResult: null }; Flow: 1. User types a product query (e.g. \"Samsung phones\") 2. Groq refines the query into specific suggestions 3. SerpAPI searches Google Shopping for matching products 4. User selects 2--5 products from results 5. Cheerio scrapes Croma / Reliance Digital product pages 6. Gemini/Groq suggests ideal values and weights 7. User confirms тЖТ existing weighted penalty algorithm runs Scraping targets: croma.com, reliancedigital.in Rationale: Both sites are server-rendered with minimal bot protection, making them more reliable than Amazon for demo use. Known limitations: - CSS selectors may drift if Croma/Reliance update their HTML structure - SerpAPI free tier: 100 searches/month - Scraped data is point-in-time; prices may change - Phase 3 will add Firebase caching to reduce re-scraping AI role in Phase 2: - Query refinement: Groq suggests better search terms (user confirms) - Ideal suggestion: Gemini/Groq suggests values (user edits before algorithm runs) - AI never touches the ranking math \`\`\`

Phase 2.5 --- AI Spec Extraction & Priorities UI Upgrade Background Since Croma/Reliance block HTML scraping, our scrapers fall back to the og:title string, which contains the spec data embedded in the name (e.g., \"Buy Lenovo Yoga Slim 7 14IMH9 83CV008YIN Intel Core Ultra 7 155H 14.5 Inch\...\"). We\'ll use Groq/Gemini to parse this into structured specs before presenting the priorities page. The Priorities UI also needs to support three evaluation modes per criterion (Numeric, Scale 1-10, Review/Text) with per-row removal. Proposed Changes Backend --- server.js New helper: extractSpecsFromTitles(products) POST Groq/Gemini: Input: array of raw scraped product names (messy og:title strings) Output JSON: { \"products\": \[ { \"rawName\": \"Buy Lenovo Yoga Slim 7 14IMH9\...\", \"cleanName\": \"Lenovo Yoga Slim 7\", \"specs\": { \"Processor\": \"Intel Core Ultra 7 155H\", \"RAM\": \"16 GB\", \"Storage\": \"512 GB SSD\", \"Display\": \"14.5 inch\", \"Battery\": \"72 Wh\", \... } } \] } Updated /api/scrape flow Scrape URLs as before (get name , price, rating, image) Call extractSpecsFromTitles() with the raw names тЖТ get cleanName + parsed specs for each product Find common spec keys (appear in тЙе50% of products) Build criteria and products_data using AI-extracted specs Call getAISuggestions() with the enriched spec matrix Return cleanName, specs, plus a new field criteriaTypes --- a map of each criterion name to its suggested type (numeric \| scale \| review ): Processor, GPU тЖТ review Price, RAM, Storage, Battery тЖТ numeric Rating тЖТ scale NOTE If Groq/Gemini fails (network issue, rate limit), falls back to the current behaviour: slug-extracted name + Price (тВ╣) and Rating only. The user can always add specs manually in the Priorities step. Frontend --- script.js Overhauled showSmartIdeals() Each criterion row renders: Header: criterion name + AI reasoning snippet Type selector (dropdown): Numeric \| Scale (1--10) \| Review Switching type dynamically swaps the ideal input field Ideal Value input --- type-aware: Numeric: \<input type=\"number\"\> --- AI pre-fills (e.g., тВ╣79990) Scale (1--10): \<input type=\"number\" min=\"1\" max=\"10\"\> --- AI pre-fills (e.g., 8) Review: \<input type=\"text\"\> --- AI pre-fills text (e.g., \"Intel Core i7 or better\") Importance (1--5): weight slider (unchanged) Better When (Lower/Higher): hidden for Review type Remove тЭМ button: clicking the button removes the row entirely from the DOM and the active criteria list Updated runSmartCalculation() Collect only the criteria rows still visible (not removed) For Review-type criteria тЖТ batch-call /api/preprocess to get AI numeric scores (reusing Phase 1.5 logic) Merge numeric + scale + AI-scored review values into products_data Call /api/calculate as before Frontend --- styles.css .criteria-type-select --- pill-style dropdown for type switcher .ideal-row-remove --- small red тЭМ button, hover turns row muted .criteria-row-removed --- fade-out animation on remove Verification Plan bash \# 1. # Prompt 147 : New changes

I have completed the summary of all Phase 2 and 2.5 changes. Below is a detailed breakdown of the functionality added, a context switching prompt for future work, and a file-wise modification log. ЁЯЪА Phase 2 & 2.5 Summary --- Smart Product Compare

1.  High-Level Summary This phase transformed the application from a manual data-entry tool into an automated Smart Comparison Engine. Users can now type a vague query (e.g., \"Samsug laptop\"), get AI-refined suggestions, find products from Croma and Reliance Digital, and have the system extract specifications automatically. Key Achievements:

-   AI-Powered Scraper Enrichment: Since retail sites block bot scraping, we implemented a best-effort scraper (meta tags, slugs, JSON-LD) paired with a Groq/Llama-3 model that \"hallucinates\" structured specs from messy product titles with high accuracy.

-   Dynamic Priorities UI: Overhauled the priority setting to allow Multi-Modal Evaluation. A user can compare a Laptop\'s Price (Numeric), Rating (Scale), and Processor (Review/Text) in a single unified table.

-   Scraper Resilience: Added graceful fallbacks for Akamai 403 errors and client-side rendered pages.

2.  ЁЯОп Context Switching Prompt (Use this prompt if you need a new AI session to understand the current state) \"The project is a Decision Companion Tool. Phase 1 implemented a weighted-penalty decision engine. Phase 2/2.5 added \'Smart Compare\'. Current Stack: Node.js (Express), Vanilla JS/CSS, Groq/Gemini APIs. Backend State: server.js handles /api/scrape which uses scrapers/ to get raw product data. It then calls extractSpecsFromTitles() (using Groq) to parse messy merchant titles into { cleanName, specs, criteriaTypes }. Frontend State: script.js manages smartState. The \'Set Priorities\' step ( showSmartIdeals) allows users to toggle evaluation types (Numeric/Scale/Review) and remove unwanted specs. Logic Flow: If a criterion is typed as \'Review\', runSmartCalculation first calls /api/preprocess to convert text descriptions (e.g., \'Core i7\') into 1-10 numeric scores before hitting the final /api/calculate engine. Known Limitation: SerpAPI is currently bypassed via manual URL input due to key issues; Croma scraping is limited to Meta/Slug data due to bot protection.\"

3.  ЁЯУВ Detailed File Modifications Backend --- Scrapers & Logic FileModifications backend/server.jsAdded /api/refine-query, /api/search, and /api/scrape. Implemented extractSpecsFromTitles (Phase 2.5) to structured specs from titles. Updated endpoints to return criteriaTypes. scrapers/cromaScraper.jsRewrite: Added targeted extraction for Akamai 403 errors. Extracts name from URL slug and price/image from OG meta tags/JSON-LD. scrapers/relianceScraper.jsRewrite: Best-effort strategy for SPA pages. Uses URL slugs for names and Regex for \"effective price\" scanning.scrapers/index.jsUnified router that detects merchant domain and calls the appropriate scraper. backend/decisionLogic.jsUpdated extractScoreFromText to handle robust JSON parsing from AI models to prevent \"Zero Point\" calculation errors. Frontend --- UI & Interaction FileModifications frontend/index.htmlAdded Header Tab Bar. Created 5 new step sections for the Smart Workflow (Search, Results, Preview, Ideals, Final). frontend/script.jsMajor Overhaul: Added smartState. Implemented showSmartIdeals() with Type Switcher (Numeric/Scale/Review) and Row Removal. Updated runSmartCalculation() to support batch AI-preprocessing for qualitative specs. frontend/styles.cssAdded styles for result cards, .criteria-type-select pill dropdowns, and .criteria-row-removed fade-out animations. Added glassmorphism loading overlay. backend/.envAdded GROQ_API_KEY and updated SERPAPI_KEY placeholders. Specific Phase 2.5 Logic (The \"Smart\" part):

-   Clean Naming: \"Buy Lenovo Yoga Slim 7 14IMH9\...\" тЖТ \"Lenovo Yoga Slim 7\"

-   Auto-Typing:

    -   Price/RAM/Storage тЖТ Defaults to Numeric

    -   Processor/GPU тЖТ Defaults to Review (parsed via AI)

    -   Rating тЖТ Defaults to Scale 1-10

wise_proud.png тФВ wise_surprised.png тФВ тФФтФАтФАтФАtests Files Passed : script.js, Package-lock.json, server.js, index-html, cromaScraper.js, index.js, relianceScraper.js

# Antigravity Prompt 149 : changes preview fix.md

**CHANGES_preview_fix.md**

**Fix: Show scraped product details in preview step + scrape accuracy log**

**ROOT CAUSE DIAGNOSIS**

**Issue 1 --- Preview shows no specs**

renderSmartPreview() in script.js only renders name, price, rating. The products_data matrix (which has all the specs) is stored in smartState.scrapeResult.products_data but never shown to the user.

**Issue 2 --- Scraping accuracy concern**

cromaScraper.js extracts specs from JSON-LD additionalProperty. Croma\'s product pages are JavaScript-rendered --- the spec table loads client-side, so the JSON-LD is often empty. The extractSpecsFromTitles() function in server.js uses Groq to *infer* specs from the product title --- e.g. \"20W\" from \"\...20W Portable Bluetooth Speaker\...\" becomes Power: 20. This works for specs mentioned in the title but misses specs like Battery Life, IP Rating, Bluetooth version.

The fix has two parts:

1.  Show the full scraped data matrix in the preview step so user can verify

2.  Label each value\'s source (\"from title\" vs \"from page\") for transparency

**CHANGE 1 --- frontend/script.js**

**Replace renderSmartPreview() entirely**

**Find:**

function renderSmartPreview(data) {

const container = document.getElementById(\'smart-preview-cards\');

container.innerHTML = \'\';

data.products.forEach((p) =\> {

const card = document.createElement(\'div\');

card.className = \'amazon-preview-card\';

const sourceBadge = p.source === \'croma\'

? \'\<span style=\"background:#e8f5e9;color:#2e7d32;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;font-size:0.72rem;font-weight:700;\"\>Croma\</span\>\'

: \'\<span style=\"background:#e3f2fd;color:#1565c0;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;font-size:0.72rem;font-weight:700;\"\>Reliance Digital\</span\>\';

card.innerHTML = \`

\<div class=\"amazon-card-inner\"\>

\${p.image ? \`\<img src=\"\${p.image}\" alt=\"\${p.name}\" class=\"amazon-thumb\" /\>\` : \'\<div class=\"amazon-thumb-placeholder\"\>??\</div\>\'}

\<div class=\"amazon-card-info\"\>

\<div class=\"amazon-card-name\"\>\${p.name} \${sourceBadge}\</div\>

\<div class=\"amazon-card-meta\"\>

\${p.price ? \`\<span class=\"amazon-price\"\>?\${p.price.toLocaleString(\'en-IN\')}\</span\>\` : \'\'}

\${p.rating ? \`\<span class=\"amazon-rating\"\>? \${p.rating}\</span\>\` : \'\'}

\</div\>

\</div\>

\</div\>

\`;

container.appendChild(card);

});

if (data.failures?.length \> 0) {

const fb = document.getElementById(\'smart-failures-block\');

fb.classList.remove(\'hidden\');

fb.innerHTML = \`\<div class=\"warning-alert\"\>?? \${data.failures.length} URL(s) failed: \${data.failures.map((f) =\> f.reason).join(\', \')}\</div\>\`;

}

}

**Replace with:**

function renderSmartPreview(data) {

const container = document.getElementById(\'smart-preview-cards\');

container.innerHTML = \'\';

const { products, products_data, criteria } = data;

// тФАтФА Summary note about data sources тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА

const noteEl = document.createElement(\'div\');

noteEl.className = \'scrape-source-note\';

noteEl.innerHTML = \`

\<span\>ЁЯУЛ Showing all fetched data below. Values marked

\<span class=\"tag-inferred\"\>inferred\</span\> were estimated from the

product title --- verify before running.\</span\>

\`;

container.appendChild(noteEl);

products.forEach((p) =\> {

const shortName = p.shortName \|\| p.name;

const productRow = products_data?.\[shortName\] \|\| {};

const sourceBadge = p.source === \'croma\'

? \'\<span class=\"source-badge croma-badge\"\>Croma\</span\>\'

: \'\<span class=\"source-badge reliance-badge\"\>Reliance Digital\</span\>\';

// Build spec rows for this product

const specRows = criteria

? criteria.map(c =\> {

const val = productRow\[c\];

const isEmpty = val === null \|\| val === undefined \|\| val === \'\';

return \`

\<tr\>

\<td class=\"spec-key\"\>\${c}\</td\>

\<td class=\"spec-val \${isEmpty ? \'spec-missing\' : \'\'}\"\>

\${isEmpty ? \'---\' : val}

\</td\>

\</tr\>

\`;

}).join(\'\')

: \'\<tr\>\<td colspan=\"2\" style=\"color:#94a3b8;font-size:0.8rem;\"\>No specs extracted\</td\>\</tr\>\';

const card = document.createElement(\'div\');

card.className = \'amazon-preview-card preview-expanded\';

card.innerHTML = \`

\<div class=\"preview-card-header\"\>

\${p.image

? \`\<img src=\"\${p.image}\" alt=\"\${p.name}\" class=\"amazon-thumb\" onerror=\"this.style.display=\'none\'\" /\>\`

: \'\<div class=\"amazon-thumb-placeholder\"\>ЁЯУж\</div\>\'}

\<div class=\"amazon-card-info\"\>

\<div class=\"amazon-card-name\"\>\${p.name} \${sourceBadge}\</div\>

\<div class=\"amazon-card-meta\"\>

\${p.price ? \`\<span class=\"amazon-price\"\>тВ╣\${p.price.toLocaleString(\'en-IN\')}\</span\>\` : \'\<span style=\"color:#94a3b8;font-size:0.82rem;\"\>Price not found\</span\>\'}

\${p.rating ? \`\<span class=\"amazon-rating\"\>тШЕ \${p.rating}\${p.reviewCount ? \` (\${p.reviewCount.toLocaleString(\'en-IN\')} reviews)\` : \'\'}\</span\>\` : \'\'}

\</div\>

\<a href=\"\${p.url}\" target=\"\_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" class=\"preview-url-link\"\>

View on \${p.source === \'croma\' ? \'Croma\' : \'Reliance Digital\'} тЖЧ

\</a\>

\</div\>

\</div\>

\<div class=\"preview-specs-section\"\>

\<div class=\"preview-specs-title\"\>

ЁЯУК Extracted Specs

\<span class=\"specs-count\"\>\${criteria ? criteria.length : 0} criteria\</span\>

\</div\>

\<table class=\"preview-specs-table\"\>

\<tbody\>

\${specRows}

\</tbody\>

\</table\>

\${criteria && criteria.some(c =\> productRow\[c\] === null \|\| productRow\[c\] === undefined)

? \`\<div class=\"missing-specs-note\"\>

тЪая╕П Missing values will use the column average in the algorithm.

You can also set them manually in the next step.

\</div\>\`

: \'\'}

\</div\>

\`;

container.appendChild(card);

});

// тФАтФА Failures тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА

if (data.failures?.length \> 0) {

const fb = document.getElementById(\'smart-failures-block\');

fb.classList.remove(\'hidden\');

fb.innerHTML = \`

\<div class=\"warning-alert\"\>

тЪая╕П \${data.failures.length} URL(s) could not be fetched:

\${data.failures.map(f =\> \`\<div style=\"font-size:0.82rem;margin-top:4px;\"\>\${f.url \|\| \'\'} --- \${f.reason}\</div\>\`).join(\'\')}

\</div\>

\`;

}

// тФАтФА Console debug log (development aid) тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА

console.group(\'\[SmartCompare\] Scraped Data Debug\');

console.log(\'Products:\', products.map(p =\> p.name));

console.log(\'Criteria:\', criteria);

console.log(\'Products Data Matrix:\', products_data);

console.log(\'Suggestions from AI:\', data.suggestions);

console.groupEnd();

}

**CHANGE 2 --- frontend/styles.css**

Add at the bottom of styles.css:

/\* тФАтФА Scrape preview expanded cards тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА \*/

.scrape-source-note {

background: #fffbeb;

border: 1px solid #fde68a;

border-radius: 8px;

padding: 10px 14px;

font-size: 0.82rem;

color: #92400e;

margin-bottom: 16px;

}

.tag-inferred {

background: #fef3c7;

border: 1px solid #fcd34d;

border-radius: 10px;

padding: 1px 7px;

font-size: 0.75rem;

font-weight: 700;

color: #b45309;

}

.preview-expanded {

padding: 0 !important;

overflow: hidden;

}

.preview-card-header {

display: flex;

gap: 14px;

align-items: flex-start;

padding: 14px 16px;

}

# Prompt 153 : What files to upload

Prompt 151 + Response 151 Good --- I have all the files. Let me diagnose both issues clearly. Issue 2 First (Root Cause) Looking at cromaScraper.js, it relies on JSON-LD (application/ld+json) for specs. But the actual Croma spec data you pasted --- \"Sound Output: 20W\", \"Battery Life: 30h\", \"IP Rating: IP67\" --- is not in JSON-LD. It\'s in a rendered HTML table that only loads after JavaScript runs. The scraper gets the static HTML and that table is empty. So what IS being extracted:

-   Name тЬЕ (from OG meta or slug --- working)

-   Price тЬЕ (regex тВ╣ scan --- working)

-   Rating тЪая╕П (hit or miss)

-   Specs тЭМ (JSON-LD is empty, real specs are JS-rendered) The Power, Channels, Color you see in Set Priorities came from Groq\'s extractSpecsFromTitles() --- it\'s hallucinating specs from the product title, not scraping them. That\'s why \"Power\" shows 20 for Marshall (from \"20W\" in the title) and 1400 for Croma Explode (from \"1400W\" in title). Correct by coincidence, not by scraping. Issue 1 --- Preview Step Not Showing Fetched Details Looking at renderSmartPreview() in script.js, the preview cards only show name, price, and rating. The specs object is never displayed. You said \"I need to see that\" --- correct, users need to verify what was actually fetched before trusting the priorities. Two Fixes Needed Fix A --- Show specs in preview cards so user can see exactly what was extracted and catch any gaps before running the algorithm. Fix B --- Add a \"scrape debug\" log so during development you can see what the scraper actually returned vs what Groq invented. Let me write both fixes now. It\'s getting specs like \"Power: 20\" and \"Power: 1400\" from Groq reading the product title --- which works for specs mentioned in the title. But Battery Life (30h), IP67, Bluetooth 5.1 --- those are NOT in the title so they\'re not being extracted at all right now. The spec table in the preview will make this immediately visible. # Prompt 157 : Sharing Context

Here\'s a crisp context document for your new chat: PROJECT: Smart Product Comparison System What it is: A web app where users paste Reliance Digital product URLs тЖТ it scrapes specs тЖТ user sets priorities/weights тЖТ decision engine scores and recommends the best product. Stack: Node.js + Express backend, vanilla JS frontend, Cheerio for scraping, Groq/Gemini for AI enrichment. File structure (key files only):

-   backend/server.js --- Express API, orchestrates scrape тЖТ enrich тЖТ suggest flow

-   backend/decisionLogic.js --- deterministic scoring engine (normalize тЖТ weighted distance)

-   backend/scrapers/relianceScraper.js --- Reliance Digital scraper (just fixed v2)

-   backend/scrapers/index.js --- routes URLs to correct scraper

-   frontend/script.js --- UI flow (search тЖТ preview тЖТ priorities тЖТ result)

-   frontend/index.html + styles.css What works:

-   Full UI flow end to end

-   Decision engine (scoring/weighting) is solid

-   Reliance Digital scraper v2 --- extracts real specs from \<li class=\"specifications-list\"\> in SSR HTML (tested on 2 pages, gets 23 specs reliably: Price, Rating, Brand, Power, Water Tank, Spin Speed, etc.)

-   JSON-LD gives name/price/rating/image cleanly What\'s broken / needs work:

-   Croma scraper still gets empty specs (JS-rendered, not SSR) --- deprioritized for now

-   extractSpecsFromTitles() in server.js was hallucinating specs from product titles when scraper returned empty --- now fixed by v2 scraper returning real data

-   JSON.parse(reply) in server.js line \~546 crashes with \"undefined\" is not valid JSON when Groq returns garbage --- needs null check fix

-   Preview step doesn\'t show scraped specs to user --- they can\'t verify what was extracted before running the engine

-   Gemini 429 rate limit errors in terminal (non-critical, Groq fallback handles it) How you can help in new chat: The user can run commands in browser DevTools console and paste results back. Specifically:

-   copy(document.documentElement.outerHTML) тЖТ gives raw SSR HTML of any page for scraper testing

-   Copy/paste terminal logs when errors occur

-   Verify actual scraped values vs what the UI shows Next priorities (suggested order):

1.  Fix the JSON.parse crash in server.js for bad Groq responses

2.  Show scraped specs in the preview step so user can verify before running engine

3.  Test v2 Reliance scraper live (user pastes 2 Reliance URLs, checks terminal logs)

4.  Improve common-spec filtering logic (currently тЙе50% threshold, might be too aggressive) Key insight about the architecture: Scraper returns ALL specs тЖТ server.js filters to specs common across тЙе50% of compared products тЖТ only those go into products_data{} тЖТ user sets weights тЖТ engine scores. So scraper should always return everything; filtering happens upstream. Paste this at the start of your new chat and it\'ll have full context. When you\'re ready to test the live scraper, just paste 2 Reliance Digital URLs and ask it to walk you through checking the terminal output step by step.

# Antigravity Prompt 165 : changes.md

**Changes --- Smart Compare Fixes**

**Fix 1 --- Toggle button disappears when row is deselected**

**File:** frontend/script.js **Where:** CSS class criteria-row-removed was collapsing the entire row including the header/button.

Change the toggleSmartRow function so it only hides the inputs section, not the header:

// REPLACE the existing toggleSmartRow window assignment in showSmartIdeals()

window.toggleSmartRow = (idx) =\> {

const row = document.getElementById(\'smart-row-\' + idx);

const btn = document.getElementById(\'smart-toggle-\' + idx);

if (!row \|\| row.dataset.identical === \'true\') return;

const isRemoved = row.dataset.removed === \'true\';

row.dataset.removed = isRemoved ? \'false\' : \'true\';

// Toggle only the inputs div, not the whole row

const inputs = row.querySelector(\'.amazon-ideal-inputs\');

const reasoning = row.querySelector(\'.amazon-ideal-reasoning\');

if (inputs) inputs.style.display = isRemoved ? \'\' : \'none\';

if (reasoning) reasoning.style.display = isRemoved ? \'\' : \'none\';

btn.textContent = isRemoved ? \'ЁЯЯв\' : \'тмЬ\';

row.style.opacity = isRemoved ? \'1\' : \'0.5\';

row.style.background = isRemoved ? \'\' : \'#f8fafc\';

};

Also add class amazon-ideal-reasoning to the reasoning div in the row template:

// FIND this line in the row.innerHTML template:

\<div style=\"font-size:0.8rem;color:#64748b;margin-bottom:8px;\"\>

// REPLACE WITH:

\<div class=\"amazon-ideal-reasoning\" style=\"font-size:0.8rem;color:#64748b;margin-bottom:8px;\"\>

**Fix 2 --- Green selected style (border + light green fill)**

**File:** frontend/styles.css **Where:** .criteria-toggle-btn and selected row state.

REMOVE the old .criteria-row-removed and add/replace these rules:

/\* REMOVE the old .criteria-row-removed block entirely, replace with: \*/

.criteria-row-removed {

opacity: 0.5;

background: #f8fafc;

border: 1px solid #e2e8f0 !important;

transition: all 0.2s ease;

}

/\* Green selected state --- shown on rows that are active (not removed, not identical) \*/

.amazon-ideal-row:not(.criteria-row-removed):not(.criteria-row-identical) {

border: 2px solid #22c55e !important;

background: #f0fdf4 !important;

}

/\* Toggle button \*/

.criteria-toggle-btn {

font-size: 1.1rem;

background: none;

border: none;

cursor: pointer;

padding: 0 6px 0 0;

line-height: 1;

transition: transform 0.15s ease;

}

.criteria-toggle-btn:hover {

transform: scale(1.2);

}

/\* Identical rows \*/

.criteria-row-identical {

opacity: 0.38;

background: #f8fafc !important;

border: 1px dashed #cbd5e1 !important;

pointer-events: none;

padding: 10px 14px !important;

}

**Fix 3 --- Priorities tab empty (extractSpecsFromTitles JSON.parse crash)**

**File:** backend/server.js **Where:** extractSpecsFromTitles() --- line const parsed = JSON.parse(reply) crashes if Groq returns malformed JSON, silently returns bare specs with no cleanName, which causes the Groq enrichment to be skipped entirely and criteria to be empty for earbuds (which have very sparse raw specs).

// REPLACE:

const parsed = JSON.parse(reply);

// WITH:

let parsed;

try {

const jsonMatch = reply.match(/\\{\[\\s\\S\]\*\\}/);

if (!jsonMatch) throw new Error(\'No JSON object found\');

parsed = JSON.parse(jsonMatch\[0\]);

} catch (parseErr) {

console.error(\'Spec extraction JSON parse failed:\', parseErr.message);

return products.map(p =\> ({ \...p, cleanName: p.name, criteriaTypes: {} }));

}

**Fix 4 --- Junk criteria (Item Code, Customer Care Phone, Country of origin, Warranty, Net Weight etc.)**

**File:** backend/server.js **Where:** After building specKeyCounts, before filtering common specs. These keys are scraped correctly but are useless for comparison.

// ADD this constant near the top of the /api/scrape handler (before specKeyCounts loop):

const JUNK_SPEC_KEYS = new Set(\[

\'Item Code\', \'Customer Care Phone\', \'Customer care Phone\', \'Customer care email\',

\'Country of origin\', \'Country of Origin\', \'Net Weight\', \'Commodity name\', \'Commodity Name\',

\'Item Length\', \'Item Width\', \'Item Height\', \'Net Quantity\',

\'Month and year of commodity first manufactured/packed/imported\',

\'Month and Year of Commodity First Manufactured/Imported/Packed\',

\'Name of Seller\', \'EAN\', \'In The Box\',

\]);

// THEN in the specKeyCounts loop, skip junk keys:

// REPLACE:

for (const \[key, val\] of Object.entries(p.specs)) {

if (val) specKeyCounts\[key\] = (specKeyCounts\[key\] \|\| 0) + 1;

}

// WITH:

for (const \[key, val\] of Object.entries(p.specs)) {

if (val && !JUNK_SPEC_KEYS.has(key)) specKeyCounts\[key\] = (specKeyCounts\[key\] \|\| 0) + 1;

}

**Fix 5 --- Spec limit raised from 8 to 20**

**File:** backend/server.js **Where:** commonSpecs slice.

// REPLACE:

.slice(0, 8)

// WITH:

.slice(0, 20)

This combined with Fix 4 (junk removal) means you get up to 20 *meaningful* specs instead of 8 specs polluted with Item Code etc.

**Summary of files changed**

  --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  **File**              **Changes**
  --------------------- ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  frontend/script.js    Fix 1: toggle doesn\'t hide button; add amazon-ideal-reasoning class

  frontend/styles.css   Fix 2: green border+fill for selected, remove broken collapsed style

  backend/server.js     Fix 3: safe JSON parse in extractSpecsFromTitles; Fix 4: junk key filter; Fix 5: slice(0,20)
  --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Antigravity Prompt 167 : changes2.md

\# Changes 2 --- Bug Fixes \-\-- \## Bug 1 --- \"New Comparison\" button leaves Manual tab visible \*\*File:\*\* \`frontend/script.js\` \*\*Where:\*\* \`resetSmart()\` function The issue: \`resetSmart()\` calls \`showAmazonStep(\'step-smart-search\')\` but never re-hides the manual tab container. The \`div#tab-manual\` has \`.hidden\` toggled by \`switchTab()\` --- but after a full flow, it gets exposed. \`\`\`js // REPLACE resetSmart(): function resetSmart() { smartState = { query: \'\', searchResults: \[\], selectedUrls: \[\], scrapeResult: null, pendingCalc: null }; document.getElementById(\'smart-query-input\').value = \'\'; document.getElementById(\'smart-suggestions\').classList.add(\'hidden\'); document.getElementById(\'smart-template\').classList.add(\'hidden\'); document.getElementById(\'smart-search-error\').classList.add(\'hidden\'); document.getElementById(\'smart-failures-block\').classList.add(\'hidden\'); document.getElementById(\'smart-preview-cards\').innerHTML = \'\'; document.getElementById(\'smart-ideals-container\').innerHTML = \'\'; document.getElementById(\'smart-results-container\').innerHTML = \'\'; // Ensure tab visibility is correct switchTab(\'smart\'); showAmazonStep(\'step-smart-search\'); } \`\`\` \-\-- \## Bug 2 --- Phones show only 7 specs, Ovens show 15+ \*\*Root cause:\*\* Phones on Reliance Digital have very sparse \`\<li class=\"specifications-list\"\>\` --- specs like Processor, RAM, Storage, Display, Battery are NOT in the spec table, they\'re only in the product title. So \`extractSpecsFromTitles()\` (Groq) must extract them from the name. The Groq enrichment IS working (you can see Processor/RAM/Storage/Display/Battery in the preview). But only 7 criteria show because: 1. \*\*Slice is still 8\*\* (if you haven\'t applied changes.md Fix 5 yet --- raise to 20) 2. \*\*The identical-value filter\*\* is greying out specs that are the same across colour variants of the same phone (e.g. 3 x S25 Ultra all have identical Processor/RAM/Storage) --- this is actually \*\*correct behaviour\*\*, those aren\'t worth comparing \*\*The real issue:\*\* You\'re comparing 3 variants of the S25 Ultra + 1 Z Fold7. Most specs are identical across the 3 S25 variants тЖТ filtered as identical. Only Price and Display/Battery differ. This is the system working correctly --- there\'s genuinely little to compare between colour variants. \*\*No code change needed for this\*\* --- the system is right. # Prompt 171 : Return Corrected Function

// тФАтФА Phase 2.5: AI Spec Extraction тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА

async function extractSpecsFromTitles(products) {

try {

const groqKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;

if (!groqKey) {

console.log(\'No GROQ key, skipping spec extraction\');

return products.map(p =\> ({ \...p, cleanName: p.name, criteriaTypes: {} }));

}

const prompt = \`You are an expert product data extractor. Your task is to process raw product data (messy titles, sparse specs) and output a standardized structured format.

Input Products:

\${products.map((p, i) =\> \`\[\${i}\] Name: \${p.name}\\nExisting Specs: \${JSON.stringify(p.specs \|\| {})}\`).join(\'\\n\\n\')}

Goal:

1\. Clean the product name into a concise \'cleanName\' (e.g. \"Lenovo Yoga Slim 7\" instead of a long SEO title).

2\. Extract key specifications from the raw name (like Processor, RAM, Storage, Display, GPU, Battery) and merge them with any Valid Existing Specs.

3\. Determine the evaluation type (\'criteriaType\') for each spec.

\- \"numeric\" = measured in numbers (e.g., RAM size, Storage size, Battery Wh).

\- \"review\" = qualitative or categorical text (e.g., Processor model, GPU model, Display tech).

\- \"scale\" = 1-10 rating (not commonly extracted from titles, but available if needed).

Output ONLY raw JSON in this exact structure, with no markdown formatting:

{

\"products\": \[

{

\"index\": 0,

\"cleanName\": \"Cleaned Product Name\",

\"specs\": {

\"Processor\": \"\...\",

\"RAM\": \"16 GB\",

\"Storage\": \"512 GB SSD\"

},

\"criteriaTypes\": {

\"Processor\": \"review\",

\"RAM\": \"numeric\",

\"Storage\": \"numeric\"

}

}

\]

}\`;

const fetch = (await import(\'node-fetch\')).default;

const response = await fetch(\'https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions\', {

method: \'POST\',

headers: { Authorization: \`Bearer \${groqKey}\`, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },

body: JSON.stringify({

model: \'llama-3.3-70b-versatile\',

max_tokens: 2000,

temperature: 0.1,

messages: \[{ role: \'user\', content: prompt }\],

}),

});

if (!response.ok) {

console.error(\'Groq api failed\', response.status);

return products.map(p =\> ({ \...p, cleanName: p.name, criteriaTypes: {} }));

}

const data = await response.json();

let reply = data.choices\[0\].message.content.trim();

// remove markdown codeblocks

if (reply.startsWith(\'\`\`\`\')) {

reply = reply.replace(/\^\`\`\`json\\n/, \'\').replace(/\\n\`\`\`\$/, \'\');

}

let parsed;

try {

const jsonMatch = reply.match(/\\{\[\\s\\S\]\*\\}/);

if (!jsonMatch) throw new Error(\'No JSON object found\');

parsed = JSON.parse(jsonMatch\[0\]);

} catch (parseErr) {

console.error(\'Spec extraction JSON parse failed:\', parseErr.message);

return products.map(p =\> ({ \...p, cleanName: p.name, criteriaTypes: {} }));

}

return products.map((p, i) =\> {

const ext = parsed.products.find(x =\> x.index === i);

if (ext) {

return {

\...p,

cleanName: ext.cleanName \|\| p.name,

specs: { \...p.specs, \...(ext.specs \|\| {}) },

criteriaTypes: ext.criteriaTypes \|\| {}

};

}

return { \...p, cleanName: p.name, criteriaTypes: {} };

});

} catch (e) {

console.error(\'Spec extraction error:\', e.message);

return products.map(p =\> ({ \...p, cleanName: p.name, criteriaTypes: {} }));

}

}

RETURN THE CORRECTED FUNCTION

# Antigravity Prompt 191 : Implement

Good --- the 503 is expected, it\'s the old SerpAPI route still running. You haven\'t patched server.js yet with the two changes I gave you. Let\'s confirm that first. Run this in your terminal:Viewed 3 filesViewed 3 filesReading script.js to understand the frontend search flowReading the truncated search/scrape section of script.jsReading the search/result rendering sectionDoneNow I have the full picture. Here\'s exactly what needs to change in script.js --- just one block: The problem In runSearch() at line 796, the frontend checks for data.serpapiUnavailable and falls back to URL paste mode. Since you\'re replacing SerpAPI with native Reliance search, this fallback logic needs to be removed and the error path cleaned up. # Prompt 192 : Verification

async function runSearch(query) {

showLoading(1);

const errorEl = document.getElementById(\'smart-search-error\');

errorEl.classList.add(\'hidden\');

try {

const res = await fetch(\'/api/search\', {

method: \'POST\',

headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },

body: JSON.stringify({ query }),

});

const data = await res.json();

hideLoading();

if (!res.ok) {

// No results found is a soft failure --- show empty grid with URL fallback

if (res.status === 404) {

renderSearchResults(\[\], query);

showAmazonStep(\'step-smart-results\');

const subtitle = document.getElementById(\'smart-results-subtitle\');

subtitle.innerHTML = \`тЪая╕П No results found for \"\<strong\>\${query}\</strong\>\" on Reliance Digital. Try a different search or paste URLs below.\`;

const details = document.querySelector(\'#smart-url-fallback details\');

if (details) details.open = true;

return;

}

errorEl.textContent = \`тЭМ \${data.error \|\| \'Search failed\'}\`;

errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\');

return;

}

smartState.searchResults = data.results;

renderSearchResults(data.results, query);

showAmazonStep(\'step-smart-results\');

} catch (e) {

hideLoading();

errorEl.textContent = \`тЭМ Network error: \${e.message}\`;

errorEl.classList.remove(\'hidden\');

}

}

\# Patch: Seed Data Fix for Reliance Scraper \*\*Date:\*\* 2026-02-28 \*\*Problem:\*\* Scraper returns \"Online Electronic Shopping Store in India\" as product name and тВ╣8,000 as wrong price because Reliance product pages need JS to render. The search API already has the correct data --- we just need to pass it through. \-\-- \## FILE 1 --- \`frontend/script.js\` \### Find this (inside \`startSmartScrape()\`): \`\`\`js body: JSON.stringify({ urls }), \`\`\` \### Replace with: \`\`\`js body: JSON.stringify({ urls, seedData: urls.map(url =\> { const match = smartState.searchResults.find(r =\> r.link === url); return match ? { url, name: match.title, price: match.priceNum, image: match.thumbnail, rating: match.rating, } : { url }; }) }), \`\`\` \-\-- \## FILE 2 --- \`backend/server.js\` \### Find this (inside \`POST /api/scrape\`, near the top of the route): \`\`\`js const { urls } = req.body; \`\`\` \### Replace with: \`\`\`js const { urls, seedData = \[\] } = req.body; \`\`\` \-\-- \### Then find this (a few lines further down in the same route): \`\`\`js const enrichedProducts = await extractSpecsFromTitles(succeeded); \`\`\` \### Replace with: \`\`\`js const enrichedProducts = await extractSpecsFromTitles(succeeded); // Merge search API seed data into products where scraper got generic fallback values enrichedProducts.forEach(p =\> { const seed = seedData.find(s =\> s.url === p.url); if (!seed) return; const genericName = !p.name \|\| p.name.includes(\'Online Electronic Shopping\') \|\| p.name.length \< 8; const wrongPrice = !p.price \|\| p.price === 8000; if (genericName && seed.name) p.name = seed.name; if (genericName && seed.name) p.cleanName = seed.name; if (wrongPrice && seed.price) p.price = seed.price; if (!p.image && seed.image) p.image = seed.image; if (!p.rating && seed.rating) p.rating = seed.rating; console.log(\`\[Scrape\] Merged seed data for: \${p.name}\`); }); \`\`\` \-\-- \## After saving both files: Nodemon will auto-restart. # Antigravity Prompt 206 : Quick Fix 2

Look at the URL difference carefully: \*\*Working (pasted URL):\*\* \`\`\` /product/asus-tuf-\...-mel0pj-9345133 \`\`\` \*\*Broken (from search API):\*\* \`\`\` /product/asus-tuf-\...-mel0pj/9345133 \`\`\` The slug from the API \*\*already contains the uid at the end\*\* (\`mel0pj-9345133\`). We\'re adding \`/{uid}\` again as a separate segment, breaking the URL. \*\*One character fix in \`relianceSearch.js\`:\*\* \*\*Find:\*\* \`\`\`js const url = (slug && uid) ? \`https://www.reliancedigital.in/product/\${slug}/\${uid}\` : null; \`\`\` \*\*Replace:\*\* \`\`\`js const url = (slug && uid) ? \`https://www.reliancedigital.in/product/\${slug}\` : null; \`\`\` Save it. Nodemon restarts. Test again --- terminal should now show \`JSON-LD Product found\` instead of \`No JSON-LD Product block found\`.
